**Gemini:** I'll search for the rEFInd installation directory and current icon files to determine which ones are being used.


**Tool Call:** `run_shell_command`
```json
{
  "description": "Read active configuration from refind.conf.",
  "command": "cat /boot/EFI/refind/refind.conf | grep -vE \"^#\" | grep -vE \"^$\""
}
```
> 
timeout 5

log_level 1


use_nvram false











resolution max


enable_mouse



use_graphics_for osx,linux,windows






scanfor manual






dont_scan_files +,vmlinuz-linux-cachyos-lts










default_selection 1







menuentry Linux {
icon EFI/refind/icons/os_linux.png

The `icons_dir` in `theme.conf` is `themes/refind-theme-regular/icons/512-192`.
Note that rEFInd paths are relative to the directory where `refind_x64.efi` is, or relative to the root of the ESP if starting with `/`.

If `include themes/refind-theme-regular/theme.conf` is used, and it's inside `/boot/EFI/refind/`, then `themes/refind-theme-regular/...` is a relative path.
